Original Riddle Analysis:
*   Original Riddle: అందరికి చెప్పి వొచ్చేది, చెప్పకుండా వెళ్ళేది? (Andariki cheppi vocchedi, cheppakunda vellēdi?) - *Comes telling everyone, goes without telling anyone?*
*   Original Answer: ప్రాణం (Prāṇam) - *Life*
*   Reasoning Pattern: The riddle describes something with two contrasting characteristics regarding its arrival and departure.
    *   Arrival: "చెప్పి వొచ్చేది" (cheppi vocchedi) - *comes telling*. A birth is an event known and announced to family and friends.
    *   Departure: "చెప్పకుండా వెళ్ళేది" (cheppakunda vellēdi) - *goes without telling*. Death often comes unexpectedly, without prior specific announcement of the exact moment.
    *   Core Logic: **Announced/Known Arrival, Unannounced/Sudden Departure.**

Here are 5 new riddles mirroring this logical structure:

**Original Riddle Logic Deconstruction:**
The original riddle describes an object that is acted upon by people in two distinct ways, but the object itself does not reciprocate those actions.
1.  **Physical Interaction:** "అందరూ నన్ను పట్టుకుంటారు కాని నేనే ఎవరిని పట్టుకొను" (Everyone holds me, but I hold no one). People physically interact with it (holding). The object is passive.
2.  **Functional Interaction:** "అందరూ నాతో మాట్లాడతారు కాని నేనే ఎవరితో మాట్లాడను" (Everyone talks with me, but I talk with no one). People use it for a specific function (communication). The object facilitates this but doesn't initiate or actively participate.

The core logic is: **"People interact with me/use me for a function X, but I do not perform/initiate X myself."**
